1b1(khri brgyad): //shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khro brgyud stong pa//bam po ldang du/
1b2(khri brgyad): rtsa gcig pa//de la nyon mongs pa med pa gang zhe no/bsam gtan la gnas
1b3(khri brgyad): nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i gnas pa/sems can
1b4(khri brgyad): gzhan dag dang /gang zag gzhan dag gi nyon mongs pa mi skye bar ting nge 'dzin gang
2a1(khri brgyad): gris 'grub pa de ni nyon mongs pa med pa zhes bya'o//de la smon nas shes pa gang zhe na/bsam gtan
2a2(khri brgyad): la gnas te 'di shes par bya'o snyam nus byang chub sems dpa' dus gsum gyi shes pa 'am/shes bya gang dang
2a3(khri brgyad): gang shes par 'dod par gyur pa de la yid kyis smon par byed cing ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas de'i smon lam de
2a4(khri brgyad): 'grub cing /shes bya de'ang shes pa de ni smon nas shes po zhes bya'o//de la mngon par shes pa drug gang zhe na//
2a5(khri brgyad): rdzu 'phrul gyi mngon par shes pa dang /lha'i mig gi mngon par shes pa dang /lha'i rna ba'i mngon par shes pa dang
2b1(khri brgyad): pha rol gyi sems shes pa'i mngon par shes pa dang /sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i mngon par shes pa dang /zag pa zad pa'i
2b2(khri brgyad): mngon par shes pa ste drug po de dag go/de la yongs su dag pa bzhi gang zhe na/ga nus yongs su dag pa dang /dmigs pa yongs su
2b3(khri brgyad): dag pa dang /thugs yongs su dag pa dang /mkhyen pa yongs su dag pa ste/bzhi po de dag go/de la dbang bcu gang zhe na/tshe la dbang
2b4(khri brgyad): ba dang /sems la dbang ba dang /yo byad la dbang ba dang /las la dbang ba dang /skye ba la dbang ba dang /mos pa la dbang ba dang /
2b5(khri brgyad): smon lam la dbang ba dang /rdzu 'phrul la dbang ba dang /ye shes la dbang ba dang /chos la dbang ba ste bcu po de dag go//rab 'byor
2b6(khri brgyad): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu gang zhe na/gnas la'ang gnas su yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen cing gnas ma yin pa
3a1(khri brgyad): la'ang gnas ma yin par yang dag pa ji lta bu bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /'das pa dang /ma 'ongs pa dang /dA ltar byung
3a2(khri brgyad): ba'i las rnams dang /las yang dag par blangs pa rnams kyi rnam par smin pa gnas kyi rnam pa dang /rgyu'i rnam par yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin
3a3(khri brgyad): du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /'jig rten gnas pa khams du ma pa dang /khams sna tshogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /
3a4(khri brgyad): sems can gzhan dag dang /gang zag gzhan rnams kyi 'dun pa du ma dang /mos pa sna tshogs yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /
3a5(khri brgyad): sems can gzhan dag dang /gang zag gzhan rnams kyi dbang po mchog dang mchog ma yin pa'i shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du
3a6(khri brgyad): rab tu mkhyen pa dang /kun tu 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /bsam gtan dang /rnam par thar pa dang /
3b1(khri brgyad): ting nge 'dzin dang /snyoms par 'jug pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dang /rnam par byang ba dang /ldang ba thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa dang /sngon
3b2(khri brgyad): gyi gnas rnam pa du ma rjes su dran te/des tshe rabs gcig kyang rjes su dran pa nas/sngon gyi gnas rnam pa du ma'i bar dag kyang rnam pa dang bcas yul phyogs dang bcas par
3b3(khri brgyad): rjes su dran pa dang /lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi'i las shin tu 'das pas sems can 'chi 'pho ba dang /skye bo dag kyang gzigs te sems can grang drag gi lus dang //
3b4(khri brgyad): ngag dang /yid kyis nyes par spyod pa dang ldan pa/log par lta ba/'phags pa rnams la skur pa 'debs pa dog rgyu de dang rkyen des lus zhig ste/shi ba'i 'og tu ngan song
3b5(khri brgyad): ngan 'gro log par lhung ba dag tu skye ba dang /sems can gang dag lus dang ngag dang yid kyis legs par spyod pa dang ldan pa yang dag par lta ba/'phags pa rnams la skur bu mi
3b6(khri brgyad): 'debs pa dag rgyu des lus zhig nas bde 'gro mtho ris kyi lha'i nang du skye ba dag kyang gzigs la/des lha'i mig rnamye par dag pa mi'i las shin tu 'das pas/sems cana'i tshe 'pho
3b7(khri brgyad): ba dang /skye ba dang /kha dog bzang ba dang /kha dog ngan pa dang /bde 'gro dang /ngan 'gro dag tu lus ji lta ba bzhin du nye bar 'gro ba dag kyang /yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen
4a1(khri brgyad): pa dang /zag pa rnams zad pa dang /zag pa myed cing sems rnam par grol ba dang /shes rab rnam par grol ba dag kyang yang dag pa ji lta ba
4a2(khri brgyad): bzhin du rab tu mkhyen pa ste/de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu zhes bya'o//rab 'byor de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi gang zhe na/de yang
4a3(khri brgyad): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so zhes dam bcas na/kye ma de la chos 'di rnams mngon par rdzogs par sangs ma rgyas so zhes lha dang bcas pa dang /bdud dang bcas
4a4(khri brgyad): pa dang /tshangs pa dang bcas pa dang /dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu'i 'jig rten na chos dang mthun par 'ga' zhig bdag la rgol lo snyam pa'i rgyu de yang dag par
4a5(khri brgyad): rjes su mi mthong ste/rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma mthong bas bde ba thob cing bag tsha ba med pa thob la/mi 'jigs pa thob ste/gnas kyis khyu mchog rlabs po che'i gnas
4a6(khri brgyad): su dam bca'o//'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par bsgrag go/tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/bram ze 'am/lha 'am/bdud dam/tshangs pa 'am/su
4a7(khri brgyad): 'ang rung bas chos dang mthun par 'jig rten du bskor mi nus pa bdag gis bskor bar bya'o zhes bya ba dang /de bzhin du sbyar te/nga zag pa zad do zhes dam bcas na/de la
4b1(khri brgyad): khyod kyis zag pa 'di dag ma zad do zhes chos dang mthun par bdag la rgol ba med pa dang /ngas gang dag bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa de dag bstan kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur
4b2(khri brgyad): ro zhes chos dang mthun par bdag la rgol ba med pa dang /ngas gang sdug bsngal yang dag par zad par byed pa/nges par 'byin pa'i lam du gsungs pa de bsten kyang sdug bsngal yang dag
4b3(khri brgyad): par zad par mi 'gyur ro zhes lha dang bcas pa dang /bdud dang bcas pa dang /tshangs pa dang bcas pa dang /dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu'i 'jig rten na chos dang mthun pa
4b4(khri brgyad): 'ga' zhig bdag la rgol lo snyam pa'i rgyu de yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ste/rgyu de yang dag par rjes su ma mthong bas bde ba thob cing /bag tsha ba med pa thob la mi 'jigs pa thob ste/
4b5(khri brgyad): gnas kyis khyu mchog rlabs po che'i gnas su dam bca'o//'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par bsgrag go/tshangs pa'i 'khor lo dge sbyong ngam/bram ze 'am/lha 'am/
4b6(khri brgyad): bdud dam/tshangs pa 'am/su 'ang rung bas chos dang mthun par 'jig rten du bskor bar mi nus pa bdag gis bskor bar bya'o zhes bya ba ste/de dag ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi zhes bya'o///
4b7(khri brgyad): rab 'byor de bzhin gshegs pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi gang zhe na/don so so yang dag par rig pa dang /chos so so yang dag par rig pa dang /nges pa'i tshig so so/
5a1(khri brgyad): yang dag par rig pa dang /spobs pa so so yang dag par rig pa'o//de dag kyang grang zhe na/don la dmigs pa dang /chos la dmigs pa dang /nges
5a2(khri brgyad): pa'i tshig la dmigs pa dang /spobs pa la dmigs pa dag go/rab 'byor de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsrung ba med pa gsum gang zhe na/de bzhin gshegs pa sku'i
5a3(khri brgyad): spyod pa yongs su dag ste/de bzhin gshegs pa la sku'i spyod pa yongs su ma dag pa mi mnga' bas gzhan dag gis ma shes na ci ma rung zhes gang bcab par dgongs pa de bzhin
5a4(khri brgyad): gshegs pa la mi mnga' ste/'di ni bsrung ba med pa dang po'o//de bzhin gshegs pa gsung gi spyod pa yongs su dag ste/de bzhin gshegs pa la gsung gi spyod pa yongs su ma
5a5(khri brgyad): dag pa mi mnga' bas gzhan dag gis ma shes na ci ma rung zhes gang bcab par dgongs pa de bzhin gshegs pa la mi mnga' ste/'di ni bsrung ba med pa gnyis pa'o//de bzhin
5a6(khri brgyad): gshegs pa thugs kyi spyod pa yongs su dag ste/de bzhin gshegs pa la thugs kyi spyod pa yongs su ma dag pa mi mnga' bas gzhan dag gis ma shes ni ci ma rung zhes gang bcab
5a7(khri brgyad): par dgongs pa de bzhin gshegs pa la mi mnga' ste/'di ni bsrung ba med pa gsum pa'o//de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i dran pa nye bar bzhag pa gsum gang zhe na/de bzhin
5b1(khri brgyad): gshegs pa chos ston pa'i tshe kha cig rna blags te gus par nyan cing bka' nyan par sems nye bar 'jog la/chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos la nan tan byed na'ang des de bzhin
5b2(khri brgyad): gshegs pa dgyes par mi 'gyur/yid bde bar mi 'gyur/thugs yang yeng por mi 'gyur te/'di ni dran pa nye bar bzhag pa dang po'o//kha cig rnami blag gus par
5b3(khri brgyad): mi nyan cing bka' nyan pa'i sems nye bar mi 'jog la/chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos la nan tan mi byed na'ang ngas de bzhin gshegs pa kun nas mnar sems su mi 'gyur/mi
5b4(khri brgyad): bzod par mi 'gyur/thugs mi ches par mi 'gyur te/'di ni dran pa nye bar bzhag pa gnyis pa'o//kha cig rna blags te gus par nyan cing bka' nyan pa'i sems nye bar 'jog la
5b5(khri brgyad): chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos la nan tan du byed/kha cig ni rna mi blag/gus par mi nyan cing bka' nyan pa'i sems nye bar mi 'jog la/chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos la nan tan
5b6(khri brgyad): mi byed na'ang des de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa 'am/kun nas mnar sems gnyis su mi 'gyur te/thams cad du dran pa dang ldan zhing mkhyen bzhin du btang snyoms su gnas pa 'di
5b7(khri brgyad): ni dran pa nye bar bzhag pa gsum pa'o//de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsnyel pa mi mnga' ba'i chos nyid gang zhe na/gang gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams don yod pa'i
6a1(khri brgyad): man du ma can ma cad rlon nga du 'as/ sa//depad+mo na
6a2(khri brgyad): gshegs pa'i bag nags kyi sgri pa smrangs pa gung zhe na/nyan du ste dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad ni rten mangs pa rnams smra sa kyang de dag la lus kyi 'gyur pa drug 'byung gi
6a3(khri brgyad): bzhin gshegs pa la ni de dag mi myunga' ste/de ni bag chags kyi sgrib pa smras pa zhis bya'o//dri la de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rje chen po gang zhe na/de bzhin gshegs pa'i
6a4(khri brgyad): thugs rje chen po gang dang ldan pas 'jig rten gyi badz+ra nye bar bzung ste/dge ba'i rtsa ba la gzigs pa'i phyir dus thams cad du sbyin lan gsum mtshan lan gsum 'jig rten la rtog pa
6a5(khri brgyad): mdzad pa ste/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs rje chen po sems can mtha' yas pa yongs su smin par bya ba la gzigs pa/rtag tu 'byung ba 'di ni thugs rje chen po zhes
6a6(khri brgyad): bya'o//rab 'byor de la sangs rgyas kyi chos mi 'dres pa bco brgyad gang zhe na/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas kyi bar du bar der
6a7(khri brgyad): de bzhin gshogs pa la 'khrul pa med pa dang /ca co me pa dang/bsgyel ba med pa dang /sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa med pa dang /tha dad pa'i 'du shes med
6b1(khri brgyad): pa dang /so sor ma brtags pa'i btang snyoms med pa dang /'dun pa nyams pa med pa dang /brtson 'grus nyams pa med pa dang /dran pa nyams pa med pa dang /ting nge 'dzin
6b2(khri brgyad): nyams pa med pa dang /shes rab nyams pa med pa dang /rnam par grol ba nyams pa med pa dang /lus kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba
6b3(khri brgyad): dang /ngag gi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang /yid kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang /'das
6b4(khri brgyad): pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa dang /ma 'ongs pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa dang /dra ltar byung ba'i dus la
6b5(khri brgyad): ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes mthong ba 'jug pa ste/de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ces bya'o//rab 'byor de bzhin ga shegs pa'i rnam pa thams cad
6b6(khri brgyad): mkhyen pa nyid gang zhe na/gang gi dmigs pa ni dngos po med pa dbang byed pa ni dran pa/rnam pa ni zhi ba/mtshan nyid ni mtshan nyid med pa ste/'di ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa
6b7(khri brgyad): nyid ces bya'o//rab 'byor de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis gang zhe na/phyag dang zhabs kyi mthil 'khor lo'i mtshan dang ldan pa dang /zhabs
7a1(khri brgyad): shin du gnas pa dang /phyag dang zhabs dra bas 'brel ba dang /phyag dang zhabs 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags pa dang /bdun mtho ba dang /sor m+bo ring ba dang /
7a2(khri brgyad): rting pa yangs pa dang /sku tshe zhing drang ba dang /zhabs la 'bar 'bur med pa dang /sku'i sru gyen du phyogs pa dang /byin pa ri dwags e ni ya'i lta bu dang /phyag sbom zhing ring ba dang /
7a3(khri brgyad): 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub pa dang /mdog gser 'dra ba dang /pags pa srab pa dang /s+phu ra rI nas skye zhing g.yas su 'khyil pa dang /zhal la mdzod spu'i mtshan mnga' ba dang /
7a4(khri brgyad): ro stod seng ge'i 'dra ba dang /dpung mgo legs par grub pa dang /thal gong rgyas pa dang /ro bro ba mkhyen po dang /shi n+ya gr-i d+ha ltar chu zheng gab pa dang /dbu gtsug tor dang ldan pa dang /
7a5(khri brgyad): ljags ring zhing srab pa dang /tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang /'gram pa seng ge'i lte bu dang tshems shin tu dkar ba dang /tshams mnyam pa dang /tshims thags bzang ba dang /tshems
7a6(khri brgyad): bzhi bcu mnga' ba dang /spyan mthon mthing dang /ba'i rdzi ma lta bu rnams so//de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag dang zhabs kyi mthil dag la 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa mu
7a7(khri brgyad): khyud can lte ba dang bcas pa/rnam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa/'di lta ste dper na rus pa 'am/ba so la gzugs su brkos pa lta bu dag mnga' bas na phyag dang zhabs
7b1(khri brgyad): 'khor lo'i mtshan dang ldan pa yin no//zhabs kyi mthil gnyis mnyam par sa la 'jog cing zhabs zhum pa med pas na zhabs shin tu gnas pa yin no//ngang ba'i rgyal po ltar phyag dang
7b2(khri brgyad): zhabs kyi sor mo dra bsre 'brel bas na phyag dang zhabs dra bas 'brel pa yin no//shing bal gyi 'dab ma ltar phyag dang zhabs 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags la skyi bas na phyag dang zhabs
7b3(khri brgyad): gzhon sha chags pa yin no//phyag dang zhabs kyi bol gnyis drang dpung mgo gnyis dang lhag pa'i phyogs mtho bos ni bdun mtho ba yin no//phyag dang zhabs kyi sor ma ring bas na sor
7b4(khri brgyad): mo ring ba yin no//zhabs kyi rting pa che bas na rting pa yangs pa yin no//khru bdun du 'phags par mtho zhing sku mi yo bas na sku che zhing drang ba yin no//pus mo'i lha nga dang /long bu shin
7b5(khri brgyad): tu mi mngon pas na zhabs 'bar 'bur med pa yin no//spu g.yas phyogs su zlum por 'khyil cing gyen du phyogs pas na sku'i spu gyen du phyogs pa yin no//byin pa ri dgas a ne
7b6(khri brgyad): ya'i byin pa dang /mda' rgyu'i snying po ltar byin gyis zlum pas na byin pa ri dgas a ne ya'i lta bu yin no//phyag sbom zhing ring ba'i phyir ma btud kyang phyag gis pus mo slebs pas
7b7(khri brgyad): na phyag sbam zhing ring ba yin no//glang po che dang rta tsong shes ltar gsang ba'i mtshan shin tu mdzes par spobs su nub pas na 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub pa yin no//gser
8a1(khri brgyad): shin tu sbyangs pa'i mdog 'dra bas na mdog gser 'dra ba yin no//pags pa gser dang dngul shin tu sbyangs pa ltar 'jam zhing sku la rdul gyis ma
8a2(khri brgyad): gos pas na pags pa srab pa yin no//spu shin tu 'byes shing gcig tu gnyis ma yin pas na s+phu re re nas skye zhing g.yas su 'khyil ba yin no//me tog kun+da dang /zla ba
8a3(khri brgyad): dang /ba'i 'o ma dang /bu mo'i mdog ltar dkar zhing /nyi ma dang zla ba brgya pas kyang shin tu 'phags par 'od gsal ba'i mdzod spus smin mtshams legs par brgyan
8a4(khri brgyad): pas na zhal la mdzod spu'i mtshan mnga' ba yin no//sku'i stod 'phel ka tsha bas na ro stod seng ge'i 'dra ba yin no//dpung mgo zlum zhing phyi lar 'dug pas na dpung mgo legs
8a5(khri brgyad): par grub pa yin no//gser gyi glegs ma shin tu rnam par phyis pa lta bus mthong ka shin du rgyas pas na thal gong rgyas pa yin no//ljags rlung dang /mkhris pa dang /bad+ma
8a6(khri brgyad): kan gyis nyams pa mi mnga' zhing /ro thams cad so sor rnam par rig pa dang /mthun par rnam par shes pas na ro bro ba mkhyen pa yin no//sku'i khrun dang /'dom gyi
8a7(khri brgyad): tshad du mnyam pas na shing n+ya gro d+hA ltar chu zheng gab pa yin no//dbu'i gtsug tor zlum zhing lham la g.yas su 'khyil ba dang ldan zhing dbu legs par grub cing lta na sdug pas
8b1(khri brgyad): na dbu gtsug tor dang ldan pa yin no//ut+pal dmar po'i 'dab ma'i mdog 'dra zhing yangs pas na ljags ring zhing srab pa yin no//dbyig gi snying po dang /byA ka la ping+ga lta bu'i
8b2(khri brgyad): gsung mnga' bas na tshangs pa'i dbyangs yin no//me long gi dkyil 'khor ltar shin tu legs par grub cing zlum la rgyas shing lta na sdug la mkhrang bas na 'gram pa seng ge lta bu
8b3(khri brgyad): yayin no//me tog kun+da dang /zla ba dang /dung gi bcag 'phro ltar shin tu dkar ba'i tshoms mnga' bas na tshems shin tu dkar ba yin no//tshems mtho driman med pas na choms
8b4(khri brgyad): mnyam pa yin no//tshems mtshams ma dod pas na tshems thags bzang ba yin no//tshems bla 'og lhag chad med cing mnyam pas na tshems bzhi bcu mnga' ba yin no///
8b5(khri brgyad): dkar gnag gi phyogs ma 'dres shing shin tu rnam par drag la/dmar po'i rgyun dang ma 'brel bas na spyan mthon mthing yin no//spyan gyi rdzi ma bla 'og legs par gzhol
8b6(khri brgyad): zhing ma 'dzings pos na de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gyi rdzi ma ni ba'i rdzi ma lta bu yin no//de la bla ma rnams la bsu bskyal dang /chos nyan pa dang /me tog phreng 'bul
8b7(khri brgyad): ba dang /gtsug lag khang dang /mchod rten la sogs pa'i gan du 'gro ba dang /g.yog 'khor gyi sbyin pa byas pas na phyog dang zhabs kyi mthil 'khor lo'i mtshan dang ldan
9a1(khri brgyad): par gyur te/de ni g.yog 'khor shin tu mang ba'i snga ltas yin no//yi dam la brtan pas na zhabs shin tu gnas par gyur te/de ni mi g.yo ba'i
9a2(khri brgyad): snga ltas yin no//bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi po sbyin pa dang /snyan par smra ba dang /don dpyod pa dang /don mthun pa dag kun tu bsten pas na phyag dang zhabs dra bas 'brel
9a3(khri brgyad): par gyur te/de ni myur du 'du ba'i snga ltas yin no//bza' ba dang /btung ba dang /bldag pa dang /bca' ba bsod pa dag gi sbyin pa byas pas na phyag dang zhabs 'jam
9a4(khri brgyad): zhing gzhon sha chags pa dang /bdun mtho bar gyur te/de gnyis ni bza' ba dang /btung ba dang /bldag pa dang /bca' ba bsod pa dag 'thob pa'i snga ltas yin no//
9a5(khri brgyad): bsad pa las thar bar byas pa dang /bza' ba dang btung ba la sogs pa byin pas srog gi rimi go byas pa dang /srog gcod pa spangs pa kun tu bsten pas na sor mo ring ba dang /
9a6(khri brgyad): rting pa yangs pa dang /sku che zhing drang bar gyur te/de dag ni sku tshe ring ba'i snga ltas yin no//dge ba'i chos yang dag par blangs pa dang /bzung ba rnams mngon par spel
9a7(khri brgyad): cing yongs su 'grib par ma byas pas na zhabs 'bar 'bur med pa dang /sku'i spu gyen du phyogs par gyur te/de gnyis ni chos yongs su mi nyams pa'i snga ltas yin no///
9b1(khri brgyad): bzo'i las dang /rig pa'i gnas rnams gus par byas shing byin pa dang /blangs pas na byin pa rI dgaswa e ne ya'i lta bur gyur te/de ni myur du 'dzin pa'i snga ltas yin no///
9b2(khri brgyad): bdog cing yod pa'i nor bslangs na med ces mi zer zhing byin pas na phyag sbom zhing ring bar gyur to/de ni dbang sbyin zhing 'dul bar byed pa'i snga ltas yin no//mdza' ba shes dang /
9b3(khri brgyad): gnyen 'dab dang /gnyen pa phan tshun 'brel ba dag gi dbyen ma byas shing /bye bar gyur pa dag bsdums pa dang /tshangs par spyod pa yang dag par blangs pa dang /gsang ba'i tshig
9b4(khri brgyad): bsrungs pas na 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub par gyur te/de ni sras mang ba'i snga ltas yin no//stan dang /gos dang /bgo ba rnams dang /khang bzangs dang /gzhal
9b5(khri brgyad): med khang dang /gnas bzang po dag gi sbyin pa byas pos na mdog gser 'dra ba dang /pags pa srab par gyur te/de gnyis ni stan dang /gos dang /bgo ba rnams dang /
9b6(khri brgyad): khang bzangs dang /gzhal med khang dang /gnas bzang po dag 'thob pa'i snga ltas yin no//'du 'dzi spangs po dang /mkhan po dang /slob dpon dang /pha ma dang /phu nul
9b7(khri brgyad): sogs pa bla ma rnams ji ltar rigs pa'i gnas su bkod cing rim gro byas pa dang /sbyin pa byin pa dang /mgu bar byas pas na spu re re nas skye zhing g.yas su 'khyil ba dang /
10a1(khri brgyad): /zhal la mdzod spu'i mtshan mnga' bar gyur te/de gnyis ni zla med pa'i spu ltas yin no//mu cor mi smra zhing gzhan la mi smod pa dang /snyan par smra ba dang /
10a2(khri brgyad): legs par smras pa la rjes su mthun par byed pa dang /seng ge'i sgra dang mthun par smra bas na ro stod seng ge'i 'dra ba dang /dpung mgo legs par grub par gyur te/de gnyis ni
10a3(khri brgyad): mi choms pa'i snga ltas yin no//nad pa rnams la rtsi dang /g.yog 'khor dang /sman dang mthun pa'i kha zas byin zhing rim gro byas pas na thal gong rgyas pa dang /ro bro ba
10a4(khri brgyad): mkhyen par gyur te/de gnyis ni gnod pa mi mnga' ba'i snga ltas yin no//kun dga'i ra ba dang /'dun sa dang /bsil khong dang /khron pa dang /bgrod dka' bar zam
10a5(khri brgyad): pa gdags pa dang /kha zas dang /me tog phreng dang /gtsug lag khang dang /'dug gnas la sogs pa bya ba la thog mAr 'gro zhing gzhan dag kyang spro ba bskyed pa dang /
10a6(khri brgyad): gzhan dag la lhag par byin pas na shing n+ya gro d+ha ltar chu zheng gab pa dang /dbu gtsug tor dang ldan par gyur to/de gnyis ni mnga'i dbang chen po brnyes pa'i snga ltos yin no//
10a7(khri brgyad): yun ring po nas 'jam zhing snyan pa dang /nyan pa'i tshig brjod pas na ljags rang zhing srab pa dang /tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan par gyur te/de gnyis ni gsung gi lam
10b1(khri brgyad): yan lag lnga dang ldan pa'i dbyangs brnyes pa'i snga ltas yin no//gsung gi lam yan lag lnga dang ldan pa'i dbyangs ni kun tu shes par bya zhing rnam par rig par bya ba dang /mnyan
10b2(khri brgyad): par 'os shing mi mthun pa med pa dang /zab cing dbyangs rjes su 'byung ba dang /mi tshugs shing rnar snyan pa dang /ma 'khrugs shing gsal ba'o//yun+da ring po nas chag
10b3(khri brgyad): bkyil pa spangs shing dus su smra bas na 'gram pa seng ge'i lta bur gyur te/de ni tshig btsun pa'i snga ltas yin no//rome gro byed pa dang /brnyas pa med pa dang /'tsho
10b4(khri brgyad): ba yongs su dag pas tshoms shin tu dkar ba dang /tshems mnyam par gyur te/de gnyis ni 'khor snga nas bsags pa'i sde ltas yin no//yun ring po nas bden zhing phra
10b5(khri brgyad): ma med par spyad pas na/tshems thags bzang ba dang /tshems bzhi bcu mnga' bar gyur te/de gnyis ni 'khor mi phyed pa'i snga ltas yin no//khyad pa dang smod par byed pa
10b6(khri brgyad): la'ang mi chags pa dang /sdang ba med cing rmongs pa med pa'i mig gis nges par rtogs pas na spyan mthon mthing dang /ba'i rdzi ma lta bur gyur te/de gnyis ni kun nas mdzes
10b7(khri brgyad): pa'i snga ltas yin no//rab 'byor de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis yin te/de dag gis rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis stong gsum gyi
11a1(khri brgyad): stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang /bzhed na 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa dag kyang snang bas khyab par mdzad do//de bzhin gshegs pa sems
11a2(khri brgyad): can rnams la thugs brtse bas 'od 'dom gang tsam du byin gyis rlob par mdzad de/gal te bcom ldan 'das kyis 'od 'dom gang bar byin gyis ma brlabs su zin na/rang bzhin
11a3(khri brgyad): gyi 'od kyis zil gyis gnon par gyur pas nyi ma dang zla ba dag gi 'od kyang mngon par mi 'gyur la/zla ba dang /zla ba phyed dang /dus tshogs dang /lo khyud khor dag kyang yod
11a4(khri brgyad): par mi 'gyur ro//rang bzhin gyi sgra dbyangs kyis kyang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mngon par go bar mdzad do//bzhed na gnyis dang /gsum dang
11a5(khri brgyad): bzhi dang ji snyed du snang bas khyab par 'gyur ba de snyed du dbyangs kyis mngon par go bar yang mdzad do//rab 'byor de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu
11a6(khri brgyad): gang zhe na 'di lta ste/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'du byed pa thams cad la ma chags po'i thugs mnga' bas na sene mo zangs kyi mdog lta bu yin/
11a7(khri brgyad): no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gnyen 'dab la byams pa bzhin du sems can la phan pa dang /bde bar dgongs pa'i thugs mnga' bas na sen mo mdog
11b1(khri brgyad): snum pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs mtho ba'i rgyud du skyes pas na sen mo mtho ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshul la kha
11b2(khri brgyad): na ma tho ba med pas na sor mo rnams zlum pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen por bsags pas na sor mo rnams rgyas pa yin no//sangs
11b3(khri brgyad): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba dag rim gyis yang dag par bsgrubs pas na sor mo rnams byin gyis phra ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku dang
11b4(khri brgyad): gsung dang thugs kyi phrin las kyi mtha' dang /'tsho ba dag shin tu dben pas ni rtsa mi mngon pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni nyon mongs pa'i mdud pa 'grol
11b5(khri brgyad): bar mdzad pas na rtsa mdud pa med pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dgongs pa shin tu dben pas na long bu mi mngon pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom
11b6(khri brgyad): ldan 'das rnams ni mi mnyam pa thams cad las 'grol bar mdzad pas na zhabs mi mnyam pa med pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi'i seng ge yin
11b7(khri brgyad): pas na seng ge'i stabs su gshegs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi'i glang po che yin pas na glang po che'i stobs su gshegs pa yin no//
12a1(khri brgyad): srangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ngang pa'i rgyal po ltar nam mkha' la bzhud pas na ngang pa'i stabs su gshegs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom
12a2(khri brgyad): ldan 'das rnams ni skyes bu'i khyu mchog yin pas nu khyu mchog gi stabs su gshegs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthun pa'i lam mnga'
12a3(khri brgyad): bas na g.yas phyogs su ldog cing gshegs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lta na mdzes pas na mdzes par gshegs pa yin no//sangs
12a4(khri brgyad): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu thugs yon po mi mnga' bas na ma yo bar gshegs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshul rnam par dag
12a5(khri brgyad): pA'i yon tan ston pas ni sku khril bag chags pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sdig pa'i chos rnams shin tu sbyangs pas na sku byi dor byas pa lta bu
12a6(khri brgyad): yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni cho snga rim gyis ston pas na sku rim par 'tsham pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku dang
12a7(khri brgyad): gsung dang thugs shin tu gtsang bas ni sku gtsang ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang bzhin gyis thugs 'jam pa dang ldan pas na sgo 'jam
12b1(khri brgyad): pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang bzhin gyis thugs rnam par dag pas na sku rnam par dag pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos/

12b3(khri brgyad): sku kho lag yangs shing bzang ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la thugs mnyam pas na gom pa snyoms pa yin no//sangs
12b4(khri brgyad): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni shin tu 'jam pa'i chos ston pas na sku shin tu gzhon mdog can yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu zhum pa med pa'i
12b5(khri brgyad): thugs mnga' bas na sku zhum pa med pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams byang bas na sku rgyas pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan
12b6(khri brgyad): 'das rnams ni yid 'byung ba'i srid par mtshams sbyor ba zad pas na sku shin tu grims pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i
12b7(khri brgyad): yan lag dang nyin lag rnams shin tu legs par ston pas na yan lag dang nying lag shin tu rnam par 'byes pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzigs
13a1(khri brgyad): pa shin tu rnam par dag pas na gzigs pa rab rib med cing rnam par dgra pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshul dang ldan pa'i
13a2(khri brgyad): slob ma mnga' bas na sku zlum pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor ba'i skyon rnams rab tu sbyangs pa su na sku skabs phyin pa yin no//sangs rgyas
13a3(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni nga rgyal gyi rtse mo bcom pas na sku ma rnyongs pa yin no//sangs rgyaso bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos zad par byed pa rnam par zlog pas na
13a4(khri brgyad): phyal phyang ngo ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos shin tu zab mo rnams thugs su chud pas na lte ba zab pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
13a5(khri brgyad): rnams ni mthun par 'dzin par zhugs pa'i slob ma mnga' bras na lta ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni slob ma kun nas
13a6(khri brgyad): mdzes pa'i dge 'dun mnga' bas na kun nas mdzes pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs shin tu gtsang bas na kun spyod pa gtsang ba yin no//
13a7(khri brgyad): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos 'dul ba nag po ston pa dang bral bas na sku la sme ba dang gnag bag med pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
13b1(khri brgyad): rnams ni shing bal ltar yang ba'i lus thob par 'gyur ba'i chos ston pas na phyag shing bal ltar shin tu 'jam pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gnyen
13b2(khri brgyad): 'dab dang /skye bo phal po che la snyoms par byams pas dge sbyong chen po yin pas na phyag gi ri mo mdangs yod pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni shin

13b4(khri brgyad): no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ha cang phal che ba ma yin pa'i bslab pa'i gzhi 'cha' ba na zhal ha cang yang mi ring ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan

13b7(khri brgyad): no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byis pa'i skye bo chags pa rnams la gting dpag dka' ba'i chos kyis 'dul bar mdzad pas ni ljags dmar ba yin no//
14a1(khri brgyad): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni glang po che'i dra ro dang /'brug gi sgra lta bus bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bas nA glang po che'i nga ro dang /'brug gi sgyu
14a2(khri brgyad): dang ldan pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni snyan cing mnyen la 'jam par smra ba'i slob ma mnga' bas na gsung snyan cing mnyen la 'jam pa yin no//sangs
14a3(khri brgyad): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni srid pa'i kun tu sbyor ba las log pas ni mche ba zlum pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni skye bo rnon po 'dul ba la mkhas
14a4(khri brgyad): pas na mche ba rno ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos 'dul ba mchog tu dkar bas na mche ba dkur ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das

14a6(khri brgyad): mche ba byin gyis phra ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni shes rab kyi ro mthon po la bzhugs pas na shangs mtho ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a7(khri brgyad): 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i skye bo gtsang ma mnga' bsen shang sa gtsang ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzigs pa rnam par dag pas na
14b1(khri brgyad): spyan rnam par dag pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pas na spyan yangs pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom
14b2(khri brgyad): ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi tshogs shin tu bsogs pas na rdzi ma sdug pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lha dang lha ma yin dang mo'i na chung
14b3(khri brgyad): mig dkar gnag 'byes shing pad+ma'i 'dab ma rangs pa lta bu dang ldan pa mchog rnams kyis mngon par dga' bar byas shing bstod pas na spyan dkar gnag 'byes shing
14b4(khri brgyad): pad+ma'i 'dab ma rangs po lta bu yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu yangs pa ston pas na smin tshugs ring ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
14b5(khri brgyad): rnams ni 'jam pos 'dul ba la mkhas pas na smin ma 'jam pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kun nas skyon mkhyen pas na smin ma'i spu mnyam pa
14b6(khri brgyad): yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sdum gyis skye bo rgyud sdum pa rnams 'dul bar mdzad pas na smin mo sdum pa yin no//sang sA rgyas
14b7(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos mchog tu yangs pa ston pas na snyan shel sdug cing ring ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni nyon mongs pa'i g.yul
15a1(khri brgyad): las rgyal bas na snyan mnyam pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems kyi rgyud ma nyams pa'i sems can 'dul bar mdzad pas
15a2(khri brgyad): na snyan gyi dbang po ma nyams pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lte bar gyur pa thams cad rnam par spangs pas na dpral ba legs par 'byes pa
15a3(khri brgyad): yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge sbyong dang /bram ze dang /phas kyi rgol ba rnams rab tu bcom pas na dpral ba dbyes che ba yin no//sangs
15a4(khri brgyad): rgyus bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam dam pa shin tu yongs su rdzogs pas na dbu shin tu rgyas pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yul la
15a5(khri brgyad): bong ba ltar dga' ba rnam par bzlog pas na dbu skra bung ba ltar gnag pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ba dang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i bag
15a6(khri brgyad): la nyal rnams spangs pas na dbu skra sdug pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgongs pa 'jam pas bstan pa'i snying po thugs su chud pas na dbu skra
15a7(khri brgyad): 'jam pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu ma 'khrugs pa'i thugs mnga' bas na dbu skra mi 'dzing ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
15b1(khri brgyad): rnams ni rtag tu mi brlang ba'i gsung mnga' bas nu dbu sgra mi bshor ba yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub kyi yan lag gi spos kyi me tog gis skye
15b2(khri brgyad): bo rnams la mthun par sgrub pas na dbu skra dri zhim pa yin no//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyag dang zhabs kyi mthil dpal be'u dang /bkra shis dang /g.yung
15b3(khri brgyad): drung 'khyil pas brgyan pa ste/rab 'byor de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la mnga' ba'i dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu yin no//rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
15b4(khri brgyad): chen po ni de ltar sbyin pa gnyis so zang zing gi sbyin pa dang /chos kyi sbyin pa dag gis sems can rnams yang dag par sdud par byed de/rab 'byor de ni byang chub sems dpa'
15b5(khri brgyad): sems dpa' chen po'i ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos yin no//rab 'byor ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos snyan par smra bas sems can rnams
15b6(khri brgyad): yang dag par sdud ce na/rab 'byor 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos pha rol tu phyin pa drug po dag gis sems can rnams yang dag par sdud par byed
15b7(khri brgyad): de/sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang /tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang /brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /bsam gtan
16a1(khri brgyad): gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /pha rol tu phyin pa drug po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos
16a2(khri brgyad): snyan par smra bas sems can rnams sdud par byed do//de ci'i phyir zhe na/pha rol tu phyin pa drug po de dag gis dge ba'i chos thams cad bsdus pa'i phyir ro//rab 'byor
16a3(khri brgyad): ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po don spyod pas sems can rnams sdud ce na/pha rol tu phyin pa drug po de dag nyid kyis 'di lta ste/sbyin pa dang /snyan

16a6(khri brgyad): shog/khyed cag yi ge mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas par gyis shig/yi ge gcig la mkhas par gyis shig/yi ge gnyis la mkhas par gyis shig/
16a7(khri brgyad): yi ge bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i bar dag la mkhas par gyis shig/yi ge gcig gis thams cad 'grib pa dang ldan par rjes su rtogs par gyis shig/yi ge gnyis
16b1(khri brgyad): kyis thams cad 'grib pa dang ldan par rjes su rtogs par gyis shig/yi ge gsum gyis thams cad 'grib pa dang ldan par rjes su rtogs par gyis shig/yi ge bzhi bcu
