16b4(khri brgyad): yin no//yi ge bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i bar dag la mkhas pa yin no//yi ge gocig tu yi ge bzhi bcu rtsa lnga 'dus par bsgom pa la mkhas pa yin no//yi ge bzhi bcu rtsa lnga
16b5(khri brgyad): rnams su yi ge gcig 'dus par bsgom pa la mkhas pa yin te/yi ge mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas par byas nas yi ge med pa mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pa yin
16b6(khri brgyad): no//rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni chos la mkhas pa dang /yi ge l-i mkhas pa yin te/de
16b7(khri brgyad): chos la mkhas pa dang /yi ge la mkhas pas chos ston te/yi ge rnams kyis yi ge med pa'i chos ston pa bzhin no//rab 'byor chos de ni yi ge med pa'i rnam
17a1(khri brgyad): bas sprul pa'o//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das glal te mtha' las 'das
17a2(khri brgyad): pa dang /thog ma dang tha ma mi mchis pa stong pa nyid kyi slad du sems can yang gtan dmigs su ma mchis la/chos kyang dmigs su ma mchis shing /chos kyi rang
17a3(khri brgyad): bzhin yang dmigs su ma mchis lags nu/bcom ldan 'das 'o na ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par smin pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyi
17a4(khri brgyad): pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang /ting nge 'dzin gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang /brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang /bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa
17a5(khri brgyad): la spyod pa dang /tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang /sbyin po'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang /bsam gton bzhi la spyod pa dang /tshad med pa bzhi
17a6(khri brgyad): la spyod pa dang /gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la spyod pa dang /byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun la spyod pa dang /stong pa nyid bcu bzhi la spyod
17a7(khri brgyad): pa dang /mtshan ma med pa dang /smon pa med pa la spyod pa dang /ting nge 'dzin rnams la spyod pa dang /rnam par thar pa brgyad la spyod pa dang /mthar gyis gnas
17b1(khri brgyad): pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la spyod pa dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang /mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang /so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang /sangs rgyas kyi
17b2(khri brgyad): chos mi 'dres pa bco brgyad dang /skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang /dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu dang /rnam par smin pa las byung ba'i mngon par shes pa drug la spyod
17b3(khri brgyad): pa ji ltar sems can rnams la chos ston par bgyid lags/de la ni sems can dang /sems can du gdags pa'ang dmigs su ma mchis lags te/sems can dmigs
17b4(khri brgyad): su ma mchis pas/gzugs kyang dmigs su ma mchis la/rnam par shes pa'i bar du'ang dmigs su ma mchis/pha rol tu phyin pa drug kyang dmigs su ma mchis
17b5(khri brgyad): la|de bzhin du dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu dang /sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi bar dag kyang dmigs su ma mchis lags so//sems can dang sems
17b6(khri brgyad): can du gdags pa dmigs su ma mchis pa de la ni gzugs kyang ma mchis la/de bzhin du dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu'i bar dag kyang ma mchis lags so//dpe byad
17b7(khri brgyad): bzang po brgyad cu'i bar dag kyang ma mchis lags na/bcom ldan 'das 'o na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa ji
18a1(khri brgyad): ltar sems can rnams la chos ston par 'gyur te/bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de sems can rnams mchis pa
18a2(khri brgyad): ma lags pa'i chos rnams la yang dag par 'dzin du stsol cing /phyin ci log la sbyor bar bgyid pa 'am/gcig tu mi 'gyur lags grang /dri ci'i slad du zhe
18a3(khri brgyad): na/bcom ldan 'das 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/byang chub sems dpa' nyid kyang mi dmigs na/
18a4(khri brgyad): byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams lta smos kyang ci 'tshal lags/de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka'
18a5(khri brgyad): stsal to//rab 'byor de de bzhin te/de de bzhin no//ji skad smras pa de bzhin te/rab 'byor sems can dmigs su med pas/nang stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//
18a6(khri brgyad): phyi stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//phyi nang stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//de bzhin du sbyar te dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi bar du rig por bya'o//phung po stong
18a7(khri brgyad): pa nyid du rig par bya'o//khams stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//skye mched stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//rten cing 'brel por 'byung ba stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//
18b1(khri brgyad): bdag stong pa nyid dang /sems can stong pa nyid dang /srog stong pa nyid dang /skye ba po stong pa nyid dang /shed las skyes pa stong pa nyid dang /gang zag stong pa nyid dang /gso ba
18b2(khri brgyad): stong pa nyid dang /byed pa po dang /byeng du 'jug pa po dang /slong ba po dang /kun nas slong ba po dang /tshor ba po dang /tshor bar byed pa po dang /shes pa po dang /mthong ba
18b3(khri brgyad): po stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//de bzhin du sbyar te bsam gtan stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//tshad med pa stong pa nyid dang /gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa stong pa
18b4(khri brgyad): nyid dang /dran pa nye bar bzhag pa stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun gyi bar dag stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//stong pa nyid stong pa nyi
18b5(khri brgyad): du rig par bya'o//mtshan ma med pa dang /smon pa med pa stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//de bzhin du sbyar te rnam par thar pa brgyad stong pa nyid dang /mthar gyis gnas pa'i
18b6(khri brgyad): snyoms par 'jug pa dgu stong pa nyid dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu stong pa nyid dang /mi 'dzegs pa bzhi stong pa nyid dang /so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi stong pa
18b7(khri brgyad): nyid dang /sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang /lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi
19a1(khri brgyad): 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa nyid dang /rang byang chub stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//byang chub sems dpa'i sa stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//
19a2(khri brgyad): sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//byang chub stong pa nyid du rig par bya'o//rab 'byor de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos de dag
19a3(khri brgyad): thams cad stong par mthong nas/phyin ci log tu gyur pa'i sems can rnams la chos ston te/ci nas kyang stong pa nyid de dag tu phyir mi ldog pa de ltar chos ston to//
19a4(khri brgyad): des chos thams cad sgrib pa med par yang dag par rjes su mthong ste/chos gang yang 'khrug par mi byed cing /gnyis su mi 'byed par yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du
19a5(khri brgyad): chos ston par byed do//rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa zhig gis sprul pa bye ba phrag du ma mngon par sprul nas kha cig ni sbyin pa la
19a6(khri brgyad): bkod/kha cig na tshul khrims la bkod cing /de bzhin du sbyar te kha cig ni bzod pa la/kha cig ni brtson 'grus la/kha cig ni ting nge 'dzin la/kha cig ni
19a7(khri brgyad): shes rab la/kha cig ni bsam gtan rnams la/kha cig ni tshad med pa rnams la/kha cig ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la/kha cig ni dran
19b1(khri brgyad): pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams la/kha cig ni 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar dag la/kha cig ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar dag la bkod/kha cig ni rgyun
19b2(khri brgyad): du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la bkod/kha cig ni byang chub kyi bar dag la bkod na/rab 'byor 'di ji snyam du sems/sprul pa des chos gang yang rnam par 'phel ba yod snyam mam//
19b3(khri brgyad): gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor rnam grangs des ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la
19b4(khri brgyad): spyod pa/sems can rnams la chos ston te/ma bcings ma grol ba'i tshul gyis de dag ni phyin ci log rnams las rnam par grol bar byed cing /de dag yang dag pa ji lta ba la 'god
19b5(khri brgyad): pa de ltar rig par bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar gzugs ni ma bcings ma grol ba yin la/tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam
19b6(khri brgyad): par shes pa'ang ma bcings ma grol ba yin te/gzugs kyi ma bcings ma grol ba nyid gang yin pa de gzugs ma ya na la/tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed
19b7(khri brgyad): rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i ma bcings ma grol ba nyid gang yin pa de'ang rnam par shes pa ma yin zhing /'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi bar gyi ma
20a1(khri brgyad): bcings ma grol ba nyid gang yin pa de'ang 'dus byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams ma yin pa'i phyir ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar
20a2(khri brgyad): gzugs dang /rnam par shes pa'i bar dag dang /'dus byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi bar gyi chos rnams ni shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro//rab 'byor byang chub
20a3(khri brgyad): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/sems can rnams la chos ston kyang sems can du dmigs pa'ang med do//byang chub sems
20a4(khri brgyad): dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis gnas te/de'ang gzugs stong zhes bya bar mi dmigs pa'i tshul dang /rnam par shes pa'i
20a5(khri brgyad): bar du stong zhes bya bar mi dmigs pa'i tshul dang /'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi bar dag stong zhes bya bar mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis gnas te/'dus
20a6(khri brgyad): byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams ni gang du'ang gnos pa'ang med do//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di ltar de dag la gang gnas par 'gyur ba'i ngo bo nyid med pas na
20a7(khri brgyad): dngos po med pa'ang dngos po med pa la mi gnas la/rang gi dngos po'ang dngos po med pa la mi gnas shing /gzhan gyi dngos po'ang dngos po med pa 'am/rang gi
20b1(khri brgyad): dngos po la mi gnas pa'i phyir ro//de ci'i phyiraro zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar de dag thams cad ni dmigs su med de/gang dmigs su med pa de ni gang la'ang gnas par mi
20b2(khri brgyad): 'gyur ba'i phyir te/rab 'byor de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/chos de dag thams cad stong pa nyid du sgom ste/rab
20b3(khri brgyad): 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang /
20b4(khri brgyad): rang sangs rgyas rnams dang /nyan thos rnams dang /'phags pa thams cad la nyes par byas pa ma yin no//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
20b5(khri brgyad): de dag dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang /rang sangs rgyas rnams dang /nyan thos rnams kyis kyang chos rnams kyi chos nyid 'di nyid rtog ste/rtogs nas kyang sems can
20b6(khri brgyad): rnams la chos ston cing /chos rnams kyi chos nyid de las kyang mi 'da' ste/chos kyi dbyings kyang 'da' ba med la/de bzhin nyid dang /yang dag pa'i mtha' yang 'da' ba med pa'i
20b7(khri brgyad): phyir ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar de dag la gang 'da' bar 'gyur ba'i rang bzhin med pa'i phyir ro////shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khri brgyad
21a1(khri brgyad): stong pa//bam po lnga bcu rtsa gnyis pa//de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang /bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//
21a2(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das gal te chos kyi dbyings la 'da' ba ma mchis shing /de bzhin nyid dang /yang dag pa'i mtha' la'ang 'da' ba ma mchis na/bcom ldan 'das 'o na ci
21a3(khri brgyad): gzugs kyang gzhan la/chos kyi dbyings kyang gzhan/de bzhin nyid kyang gzhan/yang dag pa'i mtha' yang gzhan zhig lags sam/rnam par shes pa'ang gzhan
21a4(khri brgyad): la/'dus byas dang /'dus ma byos kyi chos rnams dang /'jig rten pa dang /'jig rten las 'das pa dang /zag pa dang bcas pa dang /zag pa ma mchis pa'i
21a5(khri brgyad): chos rnams kyang gzhan pa zhig logs sam/bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor de ni ma yin te/gzugs kyang gzhan ma yin la/chos kyi dbyings kyang gzhan ma
21a6(khri brgyad): yin no//de bzhin nyid kyang gzhan ma yin la/yang dag pa'i mtha' yang gzhan ma yin no//rnam par shes pa'ang gzhan ma yin la/chos thams cad kyi bar
21a7(khri brgyad): yang gzhan ma yin no//chos kyi dbyings kyang gzhan ma yin la/de bzhin nyid dang /yang dag pa'i mtha' yang gzhan ma yin no//de skad ces bka' stsal
21b1(khri brgyad): pa dang /bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das gal te gzugs kyang gzhan ma lags shing /chos kyi dbyings kyang gzhan
21b2(khri brgyad): ma lags la rnam par shes pa'i bar yang gzhan ma lags/'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi bar yang gzhan ma lags/de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings kyi bar
21b3(khri brgyad): yang gzhan ma lags na/bcom ldan 'das 'o na nag po'i chos rnams kyi rnam par smin pa nag po ni sems can dmyal ba dang /dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang /gshin rje'i
21b4(khri brgyad): 'jig rten lags so zhes bgyi ba dang /dkar po'i chos rnams kyi rnam par smin pa dkar po ni lha dang mi rnams lags so zhes bgyi ba dang /dkar gnag gi chos rnams kyi
21b5(khri brgyad): rnam par smin pa dkar ga nag ni bde ba dang /sdug bsngal 'dres ma lags so zhes bgyi ba dang /mi gnag cing dkar ba'i chos rnams kyi rnam par smin pa mi gnag cing /
21b6(khri brgyad): dkar ba ni rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang /lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa nyid dang /rang byang chub dang /bla na med
21b7(khri brgyad): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub lags so zhes bgyi bar rnam par dgod par ji ltar 'gyur lags/de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'ongs kyis tshe dang ldan pa
22a1(khri brgyad): rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab 'byor kun rdzob kyi bden pa nye bar bzung ste/'bras bu rnam par dgod pa bstan par zad kyi/don dam pa'i
22a2(khri brgyad): bden par ni 'bras bu rnam par dgod pa bstan par mi nus so//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di lta ste/ming dang gzugs ni skye ba med pa dang /'gag pa med pa dang /kun nas
22a3(khri brgyad): nyon mongs pa med pa dang /rnam par byang ba med pa'i phyir/chos de ni rnam par rtog pa med cing bsnyad du med pa ste/de ni mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dang /thog ma dang
22a4(khri brgyad): tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do//de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang /bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das gal te kun
22a5(khri brgyad): rdzob kyi bden pa nye bar bzung ste/'bras bu rnam par dgod pa mchis kyi/don dam par ma mchis pa logs na/bcom ldan 'das 'o na byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad
22a6(khri brgyad): kyang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bur mi 'gyur lags sam/lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa nyid dang /rong byang chub dang //
22a7(khri brgyad): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mi 'gyur lags sam/de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces
22b1(khri brgyad): bka' stsal to//rab 'byor ci byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyis kun rdzob kyi bden pa 'am/don dam pa'i bden pa shes sam/'o na ni de dag la'ang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang /
22b2(khri brgyad): lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa nyid dang /rang byang chub dang /bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi 'bras bu
22b3(khri brgyad): rnam par dgod pa yod par yang 'gyur te/gal te kun rdzob kyi bden pa 'am/don dam pa'i bden po zhes bya bar shes na ni/byis la so so'i skye bo zhes bya ba'i grangs su'ang mi
22b4(khri brgyad): 'gro ba zhig na/'di ltar de dag la yongs su shes pa med de/de'i phyir de dag la rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bros bu dang /lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi 'ong ba'i
22b5(khri brgyad): 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa nyid dang /rang byang chub dang /bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi 'bras bu rnam par dgod pa dag kyang med do//rab 'byor 'di ltar
22b6(khri brgyad): byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams la ni lam yang med la/lam rnam par bzhag pa'ang meng /lam bsgom pa'ang med na/byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams la 'bras bu rnam par dgod
22b7(khri brgyad): pa lta yod par 'gyur re skan/'phags pa'i gang zag rnams la ni/lam yang yod la lam rnam par bzhag pa'ang yod/lam bsgom pa'ang yod pas na 'bras bu rnam
23a1(khri brgyad): par dgod pa'ang yod do//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das ci lam bsgom pas 'bras
23a2(khri brgyad): bu 'byung zhing 'bras bu thob par 'gyur lags sam/bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor de ni ma yin te/lam bsgom pas 'bras bu 'byung bar mi 'gyur zhing /'bras bu thob
23a3(khri brgyad): par yang mi 'gyur ro//rab 'byor lam ma bsgom par yang 'bras bu thob par mi 'gyur te/lam gyis kyang 'bras bu mi 'thob la/lam ma yin pas kyang ma yin
23a4(khri brgyad): zhing lam la mi gnas par yang ma yin te/rab 'byor de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/sems can
23a5(khri brgyad): rnams la 'bras bu rnam par 'god par byed de/chos kyi dbyings la tshar bcad pa'i tshul gyis 'bras bu rnam par 'god pa ni ma yin no//gsol pa/bcom ldan
23a6(khri brgyad): 'das gral te 'dus byas kyi khams sam/'dus ma byas kyi khams la tshar bcad pas 'bras bu rnam par dgod pa ma mchis par gyur na/bcom ldan 'das
23a7(khri brgyad): kyis 'di ni kun tu sbyor ba gsum spangs pa'i phyir/rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu yin no//'di ni 'dod pa'i 'dod chags dang /gnod sems bsrabs pa'i phyir
23b1(khri brgyad): lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yin no//'di ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba rnams spangs pa'i phyir/phyir ma 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o//'di ni gong ma'i cha
23b2(khri brgyad): dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba lnga spangs pa'i phyir dgra bcom po nyid yin no//kun 'byung ba'i chos gang ci'ang rung ba de dag thams cad 'gog pa'i chos can no zhes bya ba ni rang
23b3(khri brgyad): byang chub yin no//bag chags kyi mtsha mos sbyor ba thams cad spangs pa ni/yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub yin no zhes bka' stsal na/bcom ldan 'das 'dus
23b4(khri brgyad): byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams la tshar bcad pas 'bras bu rnam par dgod pa med do zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de bdag gis ji ltar 'tshal
23b5(khri brgyad): bar bgyi/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor ci rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu 'am/lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu 'am/phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu
23b6(khri brgyad): 'am/dgra bcom pa nyid dam/rab byang chub bam/yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dus byas yin nam/'on te 'dus ma byas pa yin/gsol pa/bcom ldan
23b7(khri brgyad): 'das de na 'dus ma bgyis rlogaso ba//bde bar gshegs pa 'dus ma bgyis legs so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor ci 'dus ma byas kyi
24a1(khri brgyad): chos la tshar gcod pa yod dam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor ci gang gi tshe rigs kyi bu 'am/rigs
24a2(khri brgyad): kyi bu mos 'dus byas sam/'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams 'di lta ste/mtshan nyid med par mtshan nyid gcig tu rtogs pa de'i tshe/'dus byas sam/'dus ma byas kyi
24a3(khri brgyad): chos gang la'ang tshar gcod par byed dam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni me lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems
24a4(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa ni 'di lta ste/nang stong pa nyid nas rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyi bar gyi tshul gyis tshar bcad pa med pa'i phyir sems
24a5(khri brgyad): can rnams la chos ston to//de sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa 'am/tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'am/bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'am/brtson 'grus kyi pha rol
24a6(khri brgyad): tu phyin pa 'am/bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'am/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'am/bsam gtan dang po nas bsam gtan bzhi pa'i bar ram/byams
24a7(khri brgyad): pa'am/snying rje 'am/dga' ba'am/btang snyoms sam/'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi bar ram/dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams sam//
24b1(khri brgyad): 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar ram/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar gyi chos gang la'ang /bdag nyid kyang mngon par zhen par mi byed la/gzhan
24b2(khri brgyad): yang mngon par zhen par mi byed do//de mngon par zhen pa med pas gang la'ang chags pa med do//'di lta ste dper na/de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa ni sbyin pa'ang sbyin
24b3(khri brgyad): par byed la sems can thams cad yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i don ma gtogs par sbyin pa'i 'bras bu la'ang chags pa med cing /sbyin pa'i 'bras bu'ang nyam sngo su
24b4(khri brgyad): myong bar mi 'gyur ro//pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi bar dag dang /zag pa dang bcas pa dang /zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi bar dang /'jig rten pa dang /'jig
24b5(khri brgyad): rten las 'das pa dang /'dus byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams gang la'ang mi gnas so//rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
24b6(khri brgyad): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'ang chos thams cad la'ang spyod la/chos gang la'ang mi gnas shing chags pa med do//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di ltar des chos
24b7(khri brgyad): rnams kyi chos kyi mtshan nyid legs par rtogs pa'i phyir ro//shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khri brgyad stong pa las/mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang /yi ge mngon
25a1(khri brgyad): par bsgrub pa bstan pa'i le'u zhes bya ste/bdun cu rtsa gsum pa'o////de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces
25a2(khri brgyad): gsol to//bcom ldan 'das ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos rnams kyi chos kyi mtshan nyid legs par rtogs pa legs/bka' stsal pa/rab
25a3(khri brgyad): 'byor dper na sprul pa 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang /gti mug la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang /gzugs la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang /rnam par shes pa'i bar la kun
25a4(khri brgyad): tu spyod pa med pa dang /de bzhin du nang dang phyi'i chos rnams la kun tu spyod po med pa dang /bgra la nyal dang /kun nas ldang ba rnams la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang /
25a5(khri brgyad): zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang //'jig rten pa dang /'jig rten las 'das pa dang /'dus byas dang /'dus ma
25a6(khri brgyad): byas kyi chos rnams la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang //lam la kun tu spyod pa med pa dang /'bras bu rnams la kun tu spyod pa med pa de ltar/rab 'byor chos rnams
25a7(khri brgyad): kyi chos kyi tshul legs par rtogs pa yin no//gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das sprul pa'i lam bsgom po ji lta bu lags/bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor
25b1(khri brgyad): lam bsgom pa gang la brten nas kun nas nyon mongs par yang mi 'gyur zhing /rnam par byang bar yang mi 'gyur la/'gro ba lnga'i 'khor ba na'ang mi snang ba yin no//
25b2(khri brgyad): gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos dngos po ma mchis pa'i chos thams cad rtogs pa lags/bcom ldan 'das kyis
25b3(khri brgyad): bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di ji snyam du sems/de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa la dngos po 'ga' zhig la brten nas kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba 'am/rnam
25b4(khri brgyad): par byang bar 'gyur ba'i dngos po gang yang dmigs su yod snyam mam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags te/bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i
25b5(khri brgyad): sprul pa la ni dngos po 'ga' zhig la brten nas kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba 'am/rnam par byang bar 'gyur ba 'am/'gro ba lnga'i 'khor ba na gda' ba'i dngos po
25b6(khri brgyad): gang yang ma mchis lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor de ltar chos rnams kyi chos kyi tshul legs par rtogs pa yin no//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe
25b7(khri brgyad): dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das ci gzugs thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa lta bu lags sam/tshor ba thams
26a1(khri brgyad): cad dang /'du shes thams cad dang /'du byed thams cad dang /rnam par shes pa thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa lta bu
26a2(khri brgyad): lags sam/rab 'byor gzugs thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa lta bu yin no//tshor ba thams cad dang /'du shes thams cad dang /'du
26a3(khri brgyad): byed thams cad dang /rnam par shes pa thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa lta bu yin no//gsol pa bcom ldan 'das gal te thams cad sprul pa
26a4(khri brgyad): lta bu lags na/sprul pa la ni gzugs ma mchis/tshor ba ma mchis/'du shes ma mchis/'du byed rnams ma mchis/rnam par shes pa ma mchis//
26a5(khri brgyad): kun nas nyon mongs pa ma mchis/rnam par byang ba ma mchis shing gang las sems can rnams yongs su thar bar bgyi ba'i 'gro ba lnga'i 'khor ba'ang ma mchis
26a6(khri brgyad): legs na/'o na ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i skyes bu'i mthur 'gyur lags/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di ji
26a7(khri brgyad): snyam du sems/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sngon byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa spyod pa na gang sems can dmyal ba'am/dud 'gro'i skye gnas
26b1(khri brgyad): sam/gshin rje'i 'jig rten nam/mi 'am lha dag las yongs su thar bar bya ba'i sems can 'ga' yang dmigs snyam mam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de na
26b2(khri brgyad): ma lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor de de bzhin no//de de bzhin te/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos gang khams gsum nas yongs su thar ba
26b3(khri brgyad): bya ba'i sems can 'ga' yang mi dmigs so//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di ltar des chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bu dang /sprul pa lta bur shes shing mthong la rnam par rig
26b4(khri brgyad): po'i phyir ro//gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bu dang /sprul pa lta bur 'tshal zhing mthong
26b5(khri brgyad): la rnam par rig lags na/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang gi don du pha rol tu phyin pa drug dang /bsam gtan bzhi dang /tshad med pa bzhi dang /gzugs
26b6(khri brgyad): med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi dang /byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun dang /byang chub kyi la me lA spyod cing /sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bgyid pa
26b7(khri brgyad): dang /sems can rnams yongs su smin por bgyid logs/de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//
27a1(khri brgyad): rab 'byor gal te sems can rnams rang rang gi chos thams cad rmi lam lta bu dang /sprul pa lta bur shes su zin na ni/byang chub sems dpa' sems
27a2(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po'ang sems can rnams kyi don du bskal pa grangs med par byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa ma spyod pa zhig na/rab 'byor 'di ltar sems can rnams rang rang
27a3(khri brgyad): gis chos thams cad rmi lam lta bu dang /sprul pa lta bur mi shes te/de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bskal pa grangs med par pha rol tu phyin
27a4(khri brgyad): pa drug la spyod cing /sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed/sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par byed do//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab
27a5(khri brgyad): 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'dis gal te chos thams cad rmi lam lta bu dang /mig yor lta bu dang /sgyu ma lta bu dang /smig rgyu lta bu dang /
27a6(khri brgyad): sprul pa lta bu lags na/bcom ldan 'das sems can rnams kyang ci la gnas na/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab gyi pha rol tu phyin pa
27a7(khri brgyad): lo spyod pas/gang las bskyod par bgyid lags/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor sems can rnams ni yod pa ma yin pa'i ming dang
27b1(khri brgyad): mtshan ma dag la gnas pas na/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas/de dag ming dang mtshan ma las bskyod par byed do//
27b2(khri brgyad): de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das mang ni gang lags/mtshan ma ni gang lags/bcom ldan 'das kyis
27b3(khri brgyad): bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ming zhes bya ba dang /mtshan ma zhes bya ba ni glo bur du ming du btags pa ste/'di lta ste ming zhes bya ba 'am/mtshan ma zhes bya ba 'am/
27b4(khri brgyad): gzugs zhes bya ba 'am/rnam par shes pa'i bar zhes bya ba 'am/bud mod ces bya ba 'am/skyes pa zhes bya ba 'am/khye'u zhes bya ba 'am/bu mo zhes bya ba 'am/
27b5(khri brgyad): sems can dmyal ba pa zhes bya ba 'am/dud 'gro'i skye gnas pa zhes bya ba 'am/gau shin rje'i 'jig rten pa zhes bya ba 'amo/lha zhes bya ba 'am/mi zhes bya ba 'am/
27b6(khri brgyad): 'dus byas kyi chos zhes bya ba 'am/'dus ma byas kyi chos zhes bya ba 'am/rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu zhes bya ba 'am/lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya
27b7(khri brgyad): ba'amo/phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya ba 'om/dgra bcom pa nyid ces bya ba 'am/rang sangs rgyas zhes bya ba 'am/yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
28a1(khri brgyad): zhes bya ba de dag ni bcos mar ming du btags pa'o//rab 'byor chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin ni ming ste/gzhol ba'i phyir ro//'dus byas thams
28a2(khri brgyad): cad ni ming tsam du zhe ni/byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams de la chags pas/de dag la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod/
28a3(khri brgyad): pa/thabs la mkhas pas 'di skad du ming 'dri ni yongs su rtog pas kun nas bskyed po yin pas/rang bzhin gyis stong zhing dngos po med pa la khyed cag yod pa ma yin
28a4(khri brgyad): par yongs su rtog pas chags par ma byed cig/mkhas pa rnams ni chos stong pa dag la mngon par zhen par mi byed do//zhes kun nas 'bral bar byed de/rab
28a5(khri brgyad): 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/thabs la mkhas pas de ltar sems can rnams la chos ston par
28a6(khri brgyad): byed do//rab 'byor mtshan ma gang zhe na/rab 'byor gnyis po 'di dag na gang la byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams chags par 'gyur ba'i mtshan ma ste/gnyis gang
28a7(khri brgyad): zhe na/gzugs kyi mtshan ma dang /gzugs med pa'i mtshan ma'o//rab 'byor de la gzugs kyi mtshan ma gang zhe na/rab 'byor gzugs gang ci'ang rung ste/
28b1(khri brgyad): rags pa 'am/phra ba 'am/bzang ba 'am/ngan pa dag ste/gang skad cig pa'i chos de dag thams cad la yongs su rtog pas 'dzin par byed pa de ni gzugs kyi mtshan ma
28b2(khri brgyad): zhes bya'o//gzugs med pa'i mtshan ma gang zhe na/gzugs med pa'i chos gang ci'ang rung ste/mtshan mar bzung zhing yongs su btags pa las nyon mongs pa skye ba de ni
28b3(khri brgyad): gzugs med pa'i mtshan ma zhes bya'o//de la byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams chags pas na/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod
28b4(khri brgyad): pa thabs la mkhas pas mtshan ma de dag dang phral nas mtshan ma med pa'i dngos po la 'dzud cing 'god par byed de/ci nas kyang 'di ni mtshan ma'o//'di ni mtshan ma med pa'o
28b5(khri brgyad): zhes gnyis su mi ltung ba de ltar 'dzud cang de ltar 'god par byed do//rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/thabs
28b6(khri brgyad): la mkhas pas de ltar sems can rnams mtshan ma dang phral nas mtshan ma med pa'i dbyings la 'dzud cing 'god par byed do//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab
28b7(khri brgyad): 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das gal te chos 'di dag thams cad de tsam du bos te/'di ltar mtshan ma ma mchis pa tsam du bas pa legs na//
29a1(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/ji ltar bdag kyang dge ba'i chos rnams kyis
29a2(khri brgyad): bye brag tu 'bogs par 'gyur la gzhan dag kyang dge ba'i chos rnams kyi bye brag tu 'bogs pa la 'god par bgyid pa dang /sa nas sa yongs su rdzogs par bgyid
29a3(khri brgyad): cing sems can rnams kyang de dag nyid la sbyor bar bgyid lags/de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka'
29a4(khri brgyad): stsal to//rab 'byor gal te mtshan ma dngos po zhig yin te/dngos po med pa ma yin par gyur na ni/rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes
29a5(khri brgyad): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/dge ba'i chos rnams kyis khyad par thob par mi 'gyur la/gzhan dag kyang khyad par 'thob pa la 'god par mi 'gyur ba zhig
29a6(khri brgyad): na/rab 'byor 'di ltar mtshan ma ni dngos po ma yin zhing /dngos po med de/rab 'byor de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha
29a7(khri brgyad): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/mtshan ma med pa'i tshul gyis/bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do//mtshan ma med pa'i tshul gyis brtson
29b1(khri brgyad): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do//de bzhin du sbyar te mtshan ma med pa'i tshul gyis bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do//tshul khrims
29b2(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do//sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do//tshad med pa rnams dang /gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug
29b3(khri brgyad): pa rnams dang /dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par byed do//'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar dag yongs su rdzogs par byed do//nang stong pa
29b4(khri brgyad): nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed do//phyi stong pa nyid yongs su rdzogs por byed do//phyi nang stong pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed do//de bzhin du sbyar te/mtshan ma med pa'i
29b5(khri brgyad): tshul gyis dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi bar dag yongs su rdzogs par byed //rnam par thar pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par byed do//mthar gyis gnas pa'i
29b6(khri brgyad): snyoms par 'jug pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par byed do//de bzhin du sbyar te/mtshan nyid med pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin gshegs po'i stobs bcu yongs su rdzogs
29b7(khri brgyad): par byed do//sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'odres pa bco brgyad kyi bar dag yongs su rdzogs par byed de/des dge ba'i chos de dag yongs su rdzogs par byas nas/mtshan ma
30a1(khri brgyad): med pa'i tshul gyis gzhan dag kyang dge ba'i chos de dag la sbyor bar byed do//rab 'byor gal te chos rnams la tha na skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas bzhag pa tsam
30a2(khri brgyad): gyi mtshan ma zhig yod par gyur na'ang /rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa mtshan ma med pa dang /dran
30a3(khri brgyad): pa med pa dang /yid la byed pa med pas chos rnams mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi 'gyur la/sems can rnams kyang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams la
30a4(khri brgyad): de bzhin nyid du 'god par yang mi 'gyur ba zhig na/rab 'byor 'di ltar chos thams cad ni zag pa med cing /mtshan nyid med pa dang dran pa med pa dang /yid la byed pa
30a5(khri brgyad): med pa yin te/rab 'byor de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyis sems
30a6(khri brgyad): can thams cad kyi don byed do//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das gal te chos thams cad
30a7(khri brgyad): mtshan ma ma mchis shing /dran pa ma mchis la yid la bgyid pa mi mchis pa lags na/bcom ldan 'das 'o na 'di dag ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos so//
30b1(khri brgyad): 'di dag ni zag pa med pa'i chos so//'di dag ni thun mong gi chos so//'di dag ni thun mong ma yin pa'i chos so//'di dag ni nyan thos kyi chos so//'di dag ni rang sangs
30b2(khri brgyad): rgyas kyi chos so//'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos so//'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos so zhes bgyi bar ji ltar bgrang bar bgyi lags/de skad ces gsol pa
30b3(khri brgyad): dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab 'byor 'di ji snyam du sems/mtshan ma med pa'ang gzhan la/nyan thos kyi
30b4(khri brgyad): chos rnams kyang gzhan zhig yin snyam mam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di ji snyam du sems/mtshan ma med
30b5(khri brgyad): pa'ang gzhan la/rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyang gzhan zhig yin snyam mam/mtshan ma med pa'ang gzhan la byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams kyang gzhan zhig yin
30b6(khri brgyad): snyam mam/mtshan ma med pa'ang gzhan la/sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyang gzhan zhig yin snyam mam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so//bka'
30b7(khri brgyad): stsol pa/rab 'byor 'o na mtshan ma med pa nyid rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang /lan cig pir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /dgra bcom pa
31a1(khri brgyad): nyid dang /rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang /byang chub sems dpa' chos rnams dang /sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yin nam/gsol pa/brtsam
31a2(khri brgyad): ldan 'das de de lta lags so//bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor rnam grangs des kyang 'di ltar chos thams cad ni mtshan ma med par rig par bya ste/rab 'byor mtshan
31a3(khri brgyad): ma med pa'i chos de dag thams cad la slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni dge ba'i chos thams cad kyis rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur te/'di
31a4(khri brgyad): lta ste pha rol tu phyin pa drug dang /bsam gtan bzhi dang /tshad med pa bzhi dang /gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi dang /dran pa nye bar bzhag
31a5(khri brgyad): pa bzhi dang /yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang /rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang /dbang po lnga dang /stobs lnga dang /byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang /'phags
31a6(khri brgyad): pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa dang /sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi bar dag gis rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di ltar byang chub
31a7(khri brgyad): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ni stong pa nyid dang /mtshan ma med pa dang /smon pa med pa'i chos rnams la bslab par bya ba ma gtogs par bslab
31b1(khri brgyad): par bya ba gzhan med pa'i phyir ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum po 'dir dge ba'i chos thams cad 'dus pa'i phyir te/'di ltar rang gi mtshan nyid
31b2(khri brgyad): stong pa nyid ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid yin no//mtshan ma dang bral ba ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo mtshan ma med pa yin no//mngon par 'du byed pa med pa ni rnam par thar
31b3(khri brgyad): pa'i sgo smon pa med pa yin te/rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum po de dag la slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de ni phung po lnga la slob pa yin/skye mched
31b4(khri brgyad): bcu gnyis la slob pa yin/khams bco brgyad la slob pa yin/gzugs me pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la slob pa yin/'phags pa'i bden pa bzho la
31b5(khri brgyad): slob pa yin/rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yan lag bcu gnyis la slob pa yin/nang stong pa nyid la slob pa yin/phyi stong pa nyid la slob pa yin/phyi nang stong pa
31b6(khri brgyad): nyid la slob pa yin/dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi bar la slob pa yin no//de bzhin du sbyar te pha rol tu phyin pa drug la slob pa yin/dran pa nye bar bzhag
31b7(khri brgyad): pa bzhi la slob pa yin/'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar la slob pa yin/de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la slob pa yin/mi 'jigs pa bzhi
32a1(khri brgyad): dang /so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang /sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la slob pa yin no//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa
32a2(khri brgyad): rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/ji ltar nye bar len
32a3(khri brgyad): pa'i phung po lnga po dag la slob pa lags/bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/
32a4(khri brgyad): gzugs rab tu shes te/gzugs ji ltar skye ba dang /gzugs ji ltar 'gog pa dang /gzugs kyi de bzhin nyid gang yin pa'ang rab tu shes so//gzugs ji
32a5(khri brgyad): ltar rab tu shes she na/'di lta ste dper na/dbu ba rdos pa la snying po med pa de bzhin du//gzugs kyang shin tu gtsa tshags dang /shin tu gsong ldong dang /
32a6(khri brgyad): shin tu snying po med par rab tu shes so//gzugs kyi skye ba ji ltar rab tu shes she na/gzugs ni gang nas kyang 'ong ba med la/gzugs ni gang du'ang 'gro ba
32a7(khri brgyad): med pas/gang nas kyang mi 'ong /gang du'ang mi 'gro ba de ltar gzugs kyi skye ba rab tu shes so//rab 'byor gang nas kyang ma 'ongs/gang du'ang ma song ba de
32b1(khri brgyad): ltar gzugs kyi skye ba dang /'jig pa rab tu shes so//gzugs kyi de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/de bzhin nyid la skye ba med pa dang /'gag pa med pa dang /
32b2(khri brgyad): 'ong ba med pa dang /'gro ba med pa dang /kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang /rnam par byang ba med pa dang /'phel ba med pa dang /'grib pa med pa de ltar de bzhin nyid
32b3(khri brgyad): rab tu shes so//rab 'byor gzhan yang de bzhin nyid ni ma nor ba de bzhin nyid yin te/de'i phyir de bzhin nyid ces bya'o//de la log pa nyid med pas de'i phyir yang de bzhin
32b4(khri brgyad): nyid ces bya ste/de ltar gzugs kyi de bzhin nyid rab tu shes so//tshor ba ji ltar rab tu shes/tshor ba'i skye ba ji ltar rab tu shes/tshor ba'i 'jig pa ji ltar rab tu shes
32b5(khri brgyad): tshor ba'i dri bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/'di lta ste dper na/chu'i chu bur gyi skye ba dang /'jig pa gsog tu 'dug pa de ltar tshor ba rab tu shes so//de gang nas
32b6(khri brgyad): kyang 'ong ba med cing /gang du'ang 'gro ba med pa da ltar tshor ba'i skye ba dang /'jig pa rab tu shes so//tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/de bzhin nyid ni
32b7(khri brgyad): ma nor ba de bzhin nyid de/de ltar tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid rab tu shes so//'du shes ji ltar rab tu shes she na/'di lta ste dper na/smig rgyu'i tshogs la chu shin tu
33a1(khri brgyad): dmigs su med pa de ltar 'du shes rab tu shes so//de gang nas kyang 'ong ba med cing gang du'ang 'gro ba med pa de ltar 'du shes kyi skye ba dang /'jig pa
33a2(khri brgyad): rab tu shes so//'du shes kyi de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid ji lta ba de ltar 'du shes kyi de bzhin nyid rab tu shos so//'du byed
33a3(khri brgyad): rnams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/'di lta ste dper na/chu shing shun pa so sor phye na snying po mi dmigs pa de ltar 'du byed rnams rab tu shes so//'du byed rnams
33a4(khri brgyad): kyi skye ba dang /'jigs pa ji ltar rab tu shes she na/de gang nas kyang 'ong ba med cing /gang du'ang 'gro ba med pa de ltar 'du byed rnams kyi skye ba dang /'jig pa rab
33a5(khri brgyad): tu shos so//'du byed rnams kyi de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid ji lta ba de ltar 'du byed rnams kyi de bzhin nyid rab tu shes so//rnam
33a6(khri brgyad): par shes pa ji ltar rab tu shes she na/'di lta ste dper na/sgyu ma mkhan gyis sprul pa'i dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa ji lta ba de ltar rnam par shes pa
33a7(khri brgyad): rab tu shes so//de gang nas kyang 'ong ba med cing /gang du'ang 'gro ba med pa de ltar rnam par shes pa'i skye ba dang 'jig pa rab tu shes so//rnam par shes
33b1(khri brgyad): pa'i de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu shes she na/tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid ji lta ba de ltar rnam par shes pa'i de bzhin nyid rab tu shes te/de ltar na rnam par shes pa'i de bzhin nyid
33b2(khri brgyad): rab tu shes pa yin no//khams rnams ji ltar shes she na/mig gi khams ni mig gi khams kyi ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar mig gi khams rab tu shes so//gzugs
33b3(khri brgyad): kyi khams ji ltar shes she na/gzugs kyi khams ni gzugs kyi khams kyi ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar gzugs kyi khams rab tu shes so//mig gi rnam par shes
33b4(khri brgyad): pa'i khams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyis ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar mig gi rnam par shes
33b5(khri brgyad): pa'i khams rab tu shes so//rna ba'i khams dang /sgra'i khams dang /rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i khams dang /sna'i khams dang /dri'i khams dang /sna'i rnam par
33b6(khri brgyad): shes pa'i khams dang /lce'i khams dang /ro'i khams dang /lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams dang /lus kyi khams dang /reg bya'i khams dang /lus kyi rnam par
33b7(khri brgyad): shes pa'i khams dang /yid kyi khams ji ltar rab tu shes she ni/yid kyi khams ni yid kyi khams kyi ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar yod kyi khams rab tu shes so//chos
34a1(khri brgyad): kyi khams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/chos kyi khams ni chos kyi khams kyi ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar chos kyi khams rab tu shes so//yid kyi rnam
34a2(khri brgyad): par shes pa'i khams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khama' ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa de ltar yid kyi
34a3(khri brgyad): rnam par shes pa'i khams rab tu shes te/de ltar na khams bco brgyud rab tu shes pa yin no//skye mched rnams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/nang gi skye mched
34a4(khri brgyad): rnams ni nang gi skye mched rnams kyis stong la/phyi'i skye mched rnams ni phyi'i skye ma med rnams kyis stong po de ltar skye mched rnams rab tu shes so//'phags pa'i bden
34a5(khri brgyad): pa rnams ji ltar rab tu shes she na/sdug bsngal 'phags pa'i bden pa rab tu shes pa dang /kun 'byung ba dang /'gog pa dang /lam 'phags pa'i bden pa
34a6(khri brgyad): rab tu shes pa'o//sdug bsngal 'phags pa'i bden par ji ltar rab tu shes she na/sdug bsngal rab tu shes pa dang /badren pa rab tu shes pa dang /'phags
34a7(khri brgyad): pa rnams kyi bden pa'o zhes rab tu shes la/gnyis las rnam par grol zhing gnyis ma yin pa ni 'phags pa'i bden pa yin par rab tu shes pa ste/kun 'byung
34b1(khri brgyad): ba'ang de bzhin/'gog pa'ang de bzhin/sdug bsngal 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang de bzhin du 'phags pa'i bden par rab tu shes so//sdug bsngal gyi de bzhin nyid
34b2(khri brgyad): ji ltar rab tu shes she na/sdug bsngal gyi de bzhin nyid ni de bzhin nyid yin pa de ltar sdug bsngal gyi de bzhin nyid rab tu shes te/de bzhin du kun 'byung ba dang /'gog pa
34b3(khri brgyad): dang /lam gyi de bzhin nyid kyang rab tu shes so//rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ji ltar rab tu shes she na/rten cing 'bral par 'byung ba ni skye ba med par rab tu shes so//
34b4(khri brgyad): de bzhin du rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba 'gag pa med pa dang /chad pa med pa dang /rtag pa med pa dang /don gcig pa ma yin pa dang /don tha dad pa ma yin pa dang /'od
34b5(khri brgyad): ba med pa dang /'gro ba med pa dang /spros pa med pa dang /zhi bar rab tu shes pa'o//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di skad ces gsol to///
34b6(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/phan tshun tha dad pa'i chos de dag de ltar rab tu 'tshal na//
34b7(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das 'o na des chos kyi dbyings rnam par dkrugs par mi 'gyur lags sam/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor gal te chos kyi dbyings su
35a1(khri brgyad): ma gtogs pa'i chos gzhan 'ga' zhig dmigs su yod na ni/rnam par dkrugs par yang 'gyur na/rab 'byor chos kyi dbyings su ma gtogs pa
35a2(khri brgyad): gang mi dmigs pas/chos kyi dbyings rnam par dkrugs par 'gyur ba'i chos gzhan ni gang yang dmigs su meng ngo //de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor chos kyi dbyings
35a3(khri brgyad): su ma gtogs pa'i chos gzhan ni de bzhin gshegs pa 'am/de bzhin gshegs pa'i nyan thos rnams kyis kyang gang yang ma dmigs pa'i phyir te/ma dmigs
35a4(khri brgyad): pas na chos kyi dbyings su ma gtogs pa'i chos gzhan 'ga' zhig dmigs su yod do zhes 'dogs par mi byed de/rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems
35a5(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas de ltar chos kyi dbyings la bslab par bya'o//de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis 'di
35a6(khri brgyad): skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi dbyings la slob pas gang la bslabs pa legs/de skad ces gsol
35a7(khri brgyad): pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ljon pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab 'byor chos kyi dbyings la bslabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
35b1(khri brgyad): sems dpa' chen po ni/chos thams cad la bslabs pa yin no//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab 'byor 'di ltar chos thams cad ni chos kyi dbyings yin pa'i phyir ro//gsol/
35b2(khri brgyad): pa/bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings lags/bka' stsal pa/rab 'byor 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung yang rung /de
35b3(khri brgyad): bzhin gshegs pa rnams ma byung yang rung /chos rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings 'di ni dbyer med pa'i tshul gyis gnas pa ste/rab 'byor chos kyi dbyings de'ang 'di lta
35b4(khri brgyad): ste/dge ba dang mi dge ba dang /'dus byas dang /'dus ma byas kyi bar gyi chos thams cad yin te/rab 'byor de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po

35b7(khri brgyad): sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ji ltar bslab par bgyi/de bzhin du ji ltar bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar brtson
36a1(khri brgyad): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lnga bslab par bgyi/ji ltar bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la
36a2(khri brgyad): bslab par bgyi/ji ltar sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bgyi/de bzhin du ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bsam gtan dang po la bslab

36a5(khri brgyad): skye mched kyi bar la bslab par bgyi/de bzhin du ji ltar dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams lnga bslab par bgyi/de bzhin du ji ltar yang dag par spong ba rnams dang /rdzu

36a7(khri brgyad): bslab par bgyi/ji ltar stong pa nyid la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar mtshan ma med pa dang /smon pa med pa la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar rnam par thar pa brgyad la
36b1(khri brgyad): bsgrub par bgyi/ji ltar snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la bslab par bgyi/de bzhin du ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu lnga bslab par bgyi/ji ltar mi 'jigs pa

36b6(khri brgyad): bslab par bgyi/ji ltar sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar bgyi ba'i slad du bslab par bgyi/ji ltar 'thab bral dang /dga' ldan dang /'phrul dga' dang /
36b7(khri brgyad): gzhon 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams dang /tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don dang /tshangs 'khor dang /'od chung dang /tshad med 'od dang /'od
37a1(khri brgyad): gsal dang /dge chung dang /tshad med dge dang /dge rgyas dang /'bras bu che dang /'du shes ma mchis pa'i sems can rnams kyi nang du skye bar
37a2(khri brgyad): bgyi ba'i slad du bslab par bgyi/ji ltar der mi skye bar bgyi ba'i slad du'ang bslab par bgyi/ji ltar gnas gtsang ma mi che dang /mi gdung dang /shin tu mthong dang /

37a6(khri brgyad): ltar rang sangs rgyas kyi sa la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sra lo bslab par bgyi/ji ltar sems can yongs su smin par bgyi ba la bslab par
37a7(khri brgyad): bgyi/ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bgyi ba la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar gzungs kyi sgo thams cad la bslab par bgyi/ji ltar ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo
37b1(khri brgyad): thams cad la bsgrub par bgyi/ji ltar gang la bslab pas chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du 'tshal bar 'gyur ba'i byang chub kyi lam la bslab par bgyi/bcom
37b2(khri brgyad): ldan 'das chos kyi dbyings la ni rnam par rtog pa de dag ma mchis te/bcom ldan 'das de'i slad du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyin ci log la spyod pa

37b6(khri brgyad): mchis te/gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings lags la/chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs lags so//rnam par shes pa'i bar nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings legs la/
37b7(khri brgyad): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa lags so//ji ltar nang gi chos bsgres pa de bzhin du chos thams cad la'ang sbar bar bgyi'o//de skad ces gsol pa dang
38a1(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab 'byor de de bzhin te/de de bzhin no//ji skad smras pa de bzhin te/

38a4(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/gal te chos kyi dbyings su ma gtogs pa'i chos 'ga' zhig mthong na ni/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
38a5(khri brgyad): byang chub la gnas par yang mi 'gyur ba zhig ni/'di ltar chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings yin te/de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab
38a6(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings su yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so//byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes
38a7(khri brgyad): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/chos de dag thams cad chos kyi dbyings su yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes nas kyang ming med pa'i chos rnams la 'di ni
38b1(khri brgyad): gzugs so//'di ni tshor ba'o//'di ni 'du shes so//'di ni 'du byed rnams so//'di ni rnam par shes pa'o//zhes bya ba dang /de bzhin du sbyar te/'dri ni byang
38b2(khri brgyad): chub po zhes bya ba'i bar du ming dang brdas ston par byed do//rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/sgyu ma mkhan nam/sgyu ma mkhan gyi slob ma mkhas pa zhig gis rdzas kyi rnam pa
38b3(khri brgyad): gang yang rung ba zhig la byin gyis brlabs nas gzugs rnam pa sna tshogs 'di lta ste/bud med kyi gzugs sam/skyes pa'i gzugs sam/glang po che'i gzugs sam//
38b4(khri brgyad): rta'i gzugs sam/glang gi gzugs sam/skyed mos tshal la mri/kun dga'i ra ba nyams dga' ba dag gam/chu klung nyams dga' ba dag gam/rdzing bu nyams dga'
38b5(khri brgyad): ba dag nye bar bstan te/der gding ba dang /rol dbyem sna tshogs bting ba dag kyang nye bar bstan nas/me tog dang me tig phreng gri yon tan dang /bza' ba dang /bca' ba
38b6(khri brgyad): ngadag kyang kun tu bstan/glu dbyangs dang rol mo mang pos skye bo dga' bar byed pa dag kyang kun tu bstan nas sbyin pa sbyin par byed pa 'am/tshul khrims srung ba 'am/bzod
38b7(khri brgyad): pa sgrub pa'am/brtson 'grus rtsom pa 'am/ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par rtse ba 'am/shes rab sgom par byed pa 'amo/des der rnam pa de lta bu dag gis rgyal rigs
39a1(khri brgyad): shing sA la chen po lta bu dag gam/bram ze'i rigs shing sA la chen po lta bu dag gam/khyim bdag gi rigs shing sA la chen po lta bu dag kyang
39a2(khri brgyad): bstan tam/rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha dag bstan tam/ri rab bstan tam/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha dag bstan tam/'thab bral lam/dga' ldan nam/
39a3(khri brgyad): 'phrul dga' 'am/gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha dag bstan tam/gzugs 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched du nye bar 'gro ba'i bar gyi lha dag bstan

39b2(khri brgyad): rnam par thar pa dang /ting nge 'dzin dang /snyoms par 'jug pa dag gis rnam par rtse ba dang /yan lag dang nying lag dag yongs su gtong ba dang /dka' ba spyod pa dang /
39b3(khri brgyad): 'jig rten gyi khams snang bar byed pa dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu sgrub par byed pa dang /mi 'dzags pa rnams dang /so so yang dag par rig pa rnams dang /
39b4(khri brgyad): byams pa chen po dang /snying rje chen po mngon par sgrub pa dag bstan tama?/sangs rgyas kyi sku yan lag dang /nying lag thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dag bstan na/de

39b7(khri brgyad): gang dag mkhas pa'i rang bzhin can/gsal zhing yid gzhungs la gzugs de dag la dpyod po dang ldan pa de dag ni 'di snyam du 'di la chos gang yang dmigs su med na/mi

40a2(khri brgyad): 'du shes pa yin no snyam pa'i shes pa 'byung ba ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos yin no snyam mo//rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes

47a4(khri brgyad): yid kyis dge ba'i chos gang ci byed kyang rung ste/sbyin po gtong ngamo/tshul khrims srung ngam/bzod pa sgrub bam/brtson 'grus rtsom mA ma/ting nge 'dzin la

47a7(khri brgyad): pa bzhi 'am/so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi 'am/byams pa chen po 'am/snying rje chen po 'am/sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dam/skyes
47b1(khri brgyad): bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis sam/dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu 'am/nyan thos kyi lam mAm/rang sangs rgyas kyi lam mamra/byang chub sems dpa'i lam

47b5(khri brgyad): pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don byed de/sems dang po bskyed pa nas bzung ste/nam du'ang bya ba ma yin pa mi byed par

49a7(khri brgyad): la/gzhan dag kyang bsam gtan bzhi pa'i bar dag la snyoms par 'jug pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug go/bdag kyang rtag par rgyun du byams pa la
49b1(khri brgyad): gnas pa yin zhing gzhan dag kyang rtag par rgyun du byams pa bsgom pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug go//bdag kyang btang snyoms kyi bar dag sgom lnga/gzhan dag kyang

158a3(khri brgyad): 'dzin pa//chu dbus 'jig par 'gyur te dogs su phyin mi 'gyur//gang zhig 'dzin pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol phyin par 'gyur//de ltar dad ldan dang ba thob pa gang zhig ni//
158a4(khri brgyad): shes rab pha rol phyin yum rjes su mi 'jug min//de dag thabs kyi yon tan shes rab yongs zin na//mchog tu rmang byung bde gshegs byang chub myur du reg/dper na
158a5(khri brgyad): la las rdza so ma btang chu skyed na//nyam chung phyir ni myur du 'jig par rig par bya//so btang bum par chu skyed lam du 'jig pa yi//'jigs pa med cing bde bar khyim du
158a6(khri brgyad): phyin par 'gyur//de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' dad pa mang gyur kyang //shes rab rnam par nyams na myur du ma rung 'gyur//dad pas shes rab kyis ni yongs su zin
158a7(khri brgyad): gyur na//sa gnyis shin tu 'das te byang chub mchog thob 'gyur//dper na bcos legs ma byas gru ni rgya mtsho'i nang //nor dang bcas shing tshong par bcas te 'dzag
158b1(khri brgyad): par 'gyur//gru de legs par bcos legs byas dang ldan gyur na//mi 'jig nor dang bcas par ngogs su phyin par gyur//de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dad pas yongs
158b2(khri brgyad): bsgos kyang //shes rab med na byang chub las ni myur nyams 'gyur//de nyid shes rab pha rol phyin pa mchog ldan na//ma smras ma nyams rgyal ba'i byang chub reg par 'gyur//
158b3(khri brgyad): lo brgya nyi shu lon te rgas shing sdug bsngal mi//langs kyang bdag nyid 'gro bar nus pa ma yin to//de ni g.yas g.yon gnyis nas mi yis brten byas na//'khyil ba'i 'jigs
158b4(khri brgyad): pa med cing bde blag 'gro bar 'gyur//de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' shes rab stobs chud pa//rab tu zhugs par gyur kyang rab tu nyams par 'gyur//de nyid thabs mkhas shes
158b5(khri brgyad): rab mchog gis yongs zin na//mi nyams de bzhin gshegs kyi byang chub reg par 'gyur//byang chub sems dpa' dang po'i las kyi sar gnas gang //lhag pa'i bsam pas
158b6(khri brgyad): sangs rgyas byang chub mchog zhugs pa//slob ma bzang po bla ma gus ldan de dag gis//bla ma mkhas pa rnams la rtag tu bsten par bya//ci phyir zhe na mkhas pa'i yon tan de
158b7(khri brgyad): las 'byung //de dag shes rab pha rol phyin pa rjes su ston//sangs rgyas chos rnams dge ba'i bshes la brten to zhes//yon tan kun gyi mchog mnga' rgyal ba de skad gsung //
159a1(khri brgyad): sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod dang de bzhin brtson 'grus dang //bsam gtan shes rab byang chub yongs su bsngo bar gyis//byang chub phung por zhen nas mchog
159a2(khri brgyad): 'dzin ma byed ces//dang po'i las can de la de skad bstan par bya//de ltar spyod pa legs 'tsho smra ba'i zla ba rnams//'gro ba'i skyabs dang dpung gnyen dang ni gnas yin te///
159a3(khri brgyad): rten dang blo dang gling dang yongs 'dren don 'don pa//gsal byed sgron ma chos mchog smra ba mi 'khrugs yin//grags chen ldan rnams bya dka' go cha gyon byed de//phung po
159a4(khri brgyad): khams dang skye mched rnams kyi go cha ma ni//theg gsum 'du shes bral zhing yongs su bzung ba med//mi ldog g.yo ba med cing mi 'khrugs chos can yin//de dag 'di
159a5(khri brgyad): 'dra'i chos dang ldan zhing spros pa med//the tshom som nyi yid gnyis bral zhing don dang ldan//shes rab pha rol phyin pa thos nas mi nur ba//gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog cing
159a6(khri brgyad): mi ldog rig par bya//'dren pa rnams kyi chos 'di zab ste mthong bar dga'//sus kyang rtogs pa med cing thob par 'gyur med pa//de phyir phan mdzod brtser ldan byang
159a7(khri brgyad): chub brnyes nas ni//sems can tshogs sus shes snyam thugs khral chung bar mdzad//sems can rnams ni gnas la dga' zhing yul rnams 'dod//'dzin la gnas
159b1(khri brgyad): shing mi mkhas blun phongs mun pa bzhin//thob par bya ba'i chos ni gnas med 'dzin med de//des na 'jig rten dag dang rtsod pa 'byung ba yin//nam mkha'i khams ni shar gyi
159b2(khri brgyad): phyogs dang lho phyogs dang //de bzhin nub kyi phyogs dang byang phyogs pa mtha' yas//steng dang 'og dang phyogs bcu'i ji snyed rnams na'ang yod//tha dad gyur pa med cing bye
159b3(khri brgyad): blabrag gyur pa mod//'das pa'i de bzhin nyid gang ma byon de bzhin nyid//da ltar de bzhin nyid gang dgra bcom de bzhin nyid//chos kun de bzhin nyid grang rgyal ba'i de bzhin
159b4(khri brgyad): nyid/chos kyi de bzhin nyid 'di thams cad bye brag med//bde gshegs byang chub tha dad chos dang bral gyur pa//'di ni byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig thob 'dod pa//thabs
159b5(khri brgyad): dang ldan pas shes rab pha rol phyin la sbyor//'dran pa'i shes rab med na thob par 'gyur ma yin//bya zhig lus che dpag tshad brgya rtsa lnga bcu par//gyur la 'dab gshog
159b6(khri brgyad): zad de nyam rtsal yod min na//de yis sum cu rtsa gsum gnas nas 'dzum gling 'dir//bdag nyid mchongs na dwer ni nyam nyes gyur pa yin//rgyal ba rnams kyi pha rol
159b7(khri brgyad): phyin pa lnga 'di yang //bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig mang por bsgrub byas shing //smon lam mtha' yas rgya chen 'jig rten rtag bsnyen kyang //thabs med shes rab bral ba
160a1(khri brgyad): nyan thos nyid du lhung //sangs rgyas theg pa 'di la nges par 'byung 'dod gang //'gro ba kun la sems snyoms pha ma'i 'du shes dang //phan pa'i sems dang /
160a2(khri brgyad): byams pa'i yid kyis brtul bya zhing //tha ba med cing drang la tshig 'jam smra bar bya//'jig rten mgon la gnas brtan rab 'byor yongs zhus pa//yon tan rgya mtsho'i nyon
160a3(khri brgyad): mongs ma mchis rtags bstan gsol//mthu che ba dag ji ltar slar ldog mi 'gyur ba//de ltar yon tan phyogs tsam rgyal bas lung bstan gsol//tha dad 'du shes
160a4(khri brgyad): bral zhing rigs pa ldan tshig smra//dge sbyong dag dang bram ze gzhan la brten mi byed//mkhas pas dus rnams rtag tu ngan song gsum po spangs//de dag dge bcu'i las
160a5(khri brgyad): kyi lam la mngon par brtson//zang zing mod par 'gro la chos ni rjes su ston//chos la gcig tu dga' zhing rtag tu tshig 'jam ldan//'gro chags nyal dang 'dug par

160b1(khri brgyad): pa 'dod pa ma yin khro bas sems dkris med//khyim par gyur kyang rtag tu dngos po gun ma chags//'tsho ba'i phyir ni ya ngas longs spyod 'tshol mi byed//drag shal spod
160b2(khri brgyad): sngags mi byed bud med sbyor sngags min//'dod pa'i las can pho mor 'gyur zhes ston mi byed//rab tu dben pa'i shes rab pha rol phyin mchog brtson//'thab dang rtsod
160b3(khri brgyad): dang bral zhing byams pa'i sems kyang brtan//kun mkhyen 'dod cing brten la rtag tu gzhol sems ldan//mtha' 'khob kla klo'i skye bo'i yul mtha' rnam par spangs//

160b5(khri brgyad): dang tshor dang 'du shes sems pa rnam shes rnams//zab ste rang bzhin mtshan ma med cing rab zhi ba//dper na mnga' yis rgya mtsho'i gting thug 'tshol po ltar//shes/

161a1(khri brgyad): btab de dang ma phrad de yi ni//nyin gcig sems kyi rnam rtog spyod pa ji snyed pa//de snyed bskal pa'i byang chub sems dpas thob par 'gyur//byang chub
161a2(khri brgyad): sems dpa' gang zhig bskal mang bya stong du//dgra bcom rang rgyal sbyin byed tshul khrims srung byed kyang //gang zhig shes rab pha rol phyin mchog ldan pa'i chos//brjod

161b2(khri brgyad): de med par yang de mi chog/me lce phrad pa tha mas snying po tshig min la//mau lce tha ma med par snying po tshig min ltar//dang po'i sems kyis byang chub mchog reg ma yin la//de
